# First Ever Radio Broadcast
country_event = {
	id = WW1_Expansion_country.1
	title = WW1_Expansion_country.1.t
	desc = WW1_Expansion_country.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WW1_Expansion_country1
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = USA
		date > 1910.1.13
		date < 1910.2.13
	}

	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_country.1.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_stability = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = WW1_Expansion_news.1
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# First Ever Radio Broadcast

	id = WW1_Expansion_news.1

	desc = WW1_Expansion_news.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_WW1_Expansion_news1

	major = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_news.1.a
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

# George V becomes King of the UK upon the death of his father, Edward VII
country_event = {
	id = WW1_Expansion_country.8
	title = WW1_Expansion_country.8.t
	desc = WW1_Expansion_country.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WW1_Expansion_country8
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		date > 1910.5.6
		date < 1910.6.6
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Edward VII"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_country.8.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_stability = -0.05
		
		retire_ideology_leader = democratic
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality
		
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "George V"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ENG/WW1/Young_George_V.dds"
			expire = "1936.1.20"
			ideology = constitutional_monarchism
		}

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "George V"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/ENG/WW1/Young_George_V.dds"
			expire = "1936.1.20"
			ideology = despotism
		}

		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				RON_is_European_Country = yes
			}
			news_event = {
				id = WW1_Expansion_news.8
				hours = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = WW1_Expansion_country.14
	title = WW1_Expansion_country.14.t
	desc = WW1_Expansion_country.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WW1_Expansion_country14
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = OTT
		date > 1910.7.24
		date < 1910.8.24
		OR = {
			owns_state = 44
			ALB = {
				is_subject_of = OTT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_country.14.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_war_support = 0.05

		news_event = {
			id = WW1_Expansion_news.14
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}

# Japan–Korea Treaty of 1910
country_event = {
	id = WW1_Expansion_country.15
	title = WW1_Expansion_country.15.t
	desc = WW1_Expansion_country.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WW1_Expansion_country15
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		date > 1910.8.22
		date < 1910.9.22
		country_exists = KOR
		OR = {
			KOR = { 
				is_subject = no 
			}
			KOR = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_country.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		release = KOR
		end_puppet = KOR
		KOR = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.1
				hours = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_country.15.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			
		}
		KOR = {
			country_event = {
				id = ron_decolonizationdiplo.26
				hours = 1
			}
		}
	}

}

# Vajiravudh (Rama VI) is crowned King of Siam, after the death of his father, King Chulalongkorn
country_event = {
	id = WW1_Expansion_country.20
	title = WW1_Expansion_country.20.t
	desc = WW1_Expansion_country.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WW1_Expansion_country20
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SIA
		date > 1910.10.23
		date < 1910.11.23
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Chulalongkorn"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = WW1_Expansion_country.20.a

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		add_stability = -0.05
		
		retire_ideology_leader = neutrality

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Vajiravudh"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/SIA/WW1/Siam_Vajiravudh.dds"
			expire = "2060.1.1"
			ideology = despotism
		}

		news_event = {
			id = WW1_Expansion_news.20
			hours = 6
		}
	}
}
